is one of the most played board games in the world, play with your friends, try to defeat your opponents with strategy, reasoning and a little bit of luck.\r\nGeneral rules of dominoes:\r\n- Blocking game\r\nThe most basic dominos variant is for two players and requires a double six set. The 28 domino tiles are shuffled face down and form the stock or boneyard. Each player draws seven tiles; the remainder are not used. Once the players begin drawing tiles, they are typically placed on-edge before the players, so that each player can see his own domino tiles, but none can see the value of other players' tiles. Every player can thus see how many tiles remain in the other players' hands at all times during gameplay. One player begins by downing (playing the first tile) one of their tiles. In different games first tiles are also different. In Muggins player should start with the highest double (6-6), in Bergen the first move should be 0-0, in Mexican train each round starts with the next lower double. This tile starts the line of play, a series of tiles in which adjacent tiles touch with matching, i.e. equal, values. The players alternately extend the line of play with one tile at one of its two ends. The game ends when one player wins by playing their last tile, or when the game is blocked because neither player can play. If that occurs, whoever caused the block gets all of the remaining player points not counting their own.\r\n- Scoring game\r\nPlayers accrue points during game play for certain configurations, moves, or emptying one's hand. Most scoring games use variations of the draw game. In Muggins (All fives) player must make the open ends of the layout add up to 5s or a multiple of five (5s, 10, 15, 20, etc.) In bergen player scores when numbers on the open ends are equal. If a player does not call \"domino\" before the tile is laid on the table, and another player says 'domino' after the tile is laid, the first player must pick up an extra domino. In Mexican train the double zero domino is scored as 50 points.\r\n- Draw game\r\nIn a draw game (blocking or scoring), players are additionally allowed to draw as many tiles as desired from the stock before playing a tile. The score of a game is the number of pips in the losing player's hand plus the number of pips in the stock. Most rules prescribe that two tiles need to remain in the stock. The Draw game is often referred to as simply \"dominos\".\r\n\r\nIf you like board games like Checkers, Mahjong, Backgammon and Chess, you will love Dominoes: Best Classic Dominoes Board hat, kann irgendwann schon mal den Überblick verlieren, welche Filme da überhaupt alle im Regal stehen. Mit dieser App kann man schnell und einfach eine eigene Datenbank für seine Filme aufbauen.\r\n\r\nDas Ganze funktioniert so:\r\n1.) Registriere Dich über die App, bestätige den Account und logge Dich dann ein. Je nachdem, ob man z. B. mit der ganzen Familie einen Account teilen möchte, kann man hier natürlich auch einen solchen Account anlegen.\r\n\r\n2.) Das System erfasst dann über den BarCode auf der Hülle der Bluray, DVD, etc. den Film. \r\nIn der App kann man diesen per Barcode-Scanner direkt auslesen. Das funktioniert sowohl auf dem Smartphone als auch über den Laptop oder den Computer mit Webcam.\r\n\r\n3.) Das System sucht nun nach entsprechenden Informationen wie z. B. Name, Beschreibung, Altersfreigabe, Kategorie, Bewertung, usw. und trägt diese Informationen schonmal vorab ein.\r\n\r\n4.) Speichert man diesen Eintrag, erhält man eine (für den Account) eindeutige Nummer. \r\nWir empfehlen, diese z. B. über eine Labelmaschine oder Aufkleber auf den Bluray-Hüllen (etc.) aufzutragen und sie im Schrank entsprechend zu sortieren.\r\n\r\nSucht man nun z. B. am Abend nach einem Film, kann man sich entweder durch die App einen nach bestimmten Kriterien vorschlagen lassen oder über die Suchfunktion an Hand von verschiedenen Kriterien einen Film aussuchen. Durch die eindeutige Nummer (ID), kann man diesen Film dann schnell und einfach aus seiner Sammlung ziehen und seinen Film geniesen.\r\n\r\nDa die App auch auf Smartphones läuft, kann man z. B. auch im Laden nachschauen, ob der Film bereits in der Sammlung auftaucht oder ob es sich um einen neuen Film handelt. Das ist besonders wichtig, wenn man die Filmsammlung mit der Familie teilt. Nun zieht man das Smartphone, scannt den Barcode ein und sieht sofort, ob der Film bereits von einem anderen Familienmitglied gekauft wurde oder ob es ein neuer Film für die Sammlung ist. Doppelte Käufe gehören so der Vergangenheit an.\r\n\r\nWas die App für den Nutzer tun kann:\r\n- Einen Film (frei oder nach bestimmten Kritierien) vorschlagen lassen.\r\n- Nachprüfen, ob ein Film bereits Teil der Sammlung ist.\r\n- Filme an Hand unterschiedlicher Kriterien aus der Liste suchen.\r\n- In Verbindung mit einer entsprechenden Sortierung einen schnellen Zugriff auf die entsprechenden Filme bieten.\r\n\r\nHäufig gestellte Fragen zur App:\r\nIst meine Filmdatenbank dann offline verfügbar?\r\nNein. Die Daten werden auf einem deutschen Server gespeichert und sind nur mit Verbindung zum Internet abrufbar. (sonst ist es u. a. nicht möglich, den immer aktuellen Stand der Datenbank auf seinem Smartphone zu haben und es könnte vorkommen, dass man einen Film doch doppelt kauft)\r\n\r\nKann ich Filme hochladen, um sie dann über die Datenbank zu streamen?\r\nNein. Die Datenbank hilft dabei den Überblick über Filme (usw.) zu behalten, speichert aber keine Filmdaten an sich.\r\n\r\nKann ich die App auf anderen Betriebssystemen verwenden?\r\nZur Zeit geht das nur auf Windows-Systemen. Weitere Systeme sind in Planung. Bis dahin sollte man die Website verwenden. Schau also zuerst mal in Deinen Spam-Ordner. So oder so empfehle ich deshalb aber eine andere E-Mail-Adresse zu verwenden. Gut funktionieren web-, gmx-, 1und1-, telekom- und viele andere Email-Adressen. Leider kann ich gegen diese Übermittlungsprobleme nichts unternehmen. Scheinbar gab es ein Spam-Problem mit einem anderen Strato-Server, woraufhin Microsoft einfach alles Strato-Server (oder einen großen Teil) geblockt hat. ","AvailableDevicesNarratorText":"PC,HoloLens","TypeTag":"app","RecommendationReason":"","LongDescription":"Paint Arena:  The first ever Windows Mixed Reality app that lets people of all ages paint in 3D or play paintball in a shared social experience with voice chat, on both HoloLens and Immersive headsets from all over the world. NEW: AI Robot \"Pablo\" will walk you through the basics. \r\n\r\nTeleport around, explore the arena, have a conversation, or do a silly dance together. Once you are ready, join into the arena for a casual game. Simply guess what someone else is drawing or draw something for others to guess. \r\n\r\nFeeling energy for action? Try our multiplayer MR Paintball, splatter your friends or the arena with lovely colors. Remember to dodge and refill!\r\n\r\nFollow us on Twitter at https://twitter.com/Paint_Arena and share videos or screenshots of your best 3D paintings or MR paintball games with hashtag #Paint_Arena :)\r\n\r\nConceptualization: \r\nMany virtual reality games today are designed to enhance graphic intensity and immersion, but increasingly isolate the players. We believe Windows Mixed Reality can be much more than that. We decided to design a casual game that people of all ages can play, share, and socialize in mixed reality. We were inspired by a classic interactive puzzle game for friends and family, while we were amazed by the potential of the mixed reality motion controllers, so Paint Arena was born. Many thanks to Mixed Reality Academy for the paint brush example.  \r\n\r\nInstructions:\r\nYou will need a HoloLens or a WMR immersive headset with a mixed reality motion controllers (and headphones, if not Samsung Odyssey) to enjoy this experience.\r\n\r\nThis social experience is best enjoyed in a casual standing pose. If you feel you are not at the right height after app launch, simply stand up, look forward, and say or tap \"Reset Floor Level\". \r\n\r\nYou could draw and talk to others and guess each others' drawings. If you are the first one to join, you would be assigned the drawer for the first round. You would be given a random word. Draw something to help others guess the word (without drawing any letters or digits). Once someone guesses your word correctly, a guesser will chosen at random to become the drawer. \r\n\r\nToggle \"Painting On\" to \"Paint Balling\" to start shooting paintballs and splatter the arena. Each full tank contains 100 paintballs. Every 5 seconds, you can partially refill the tank with 20 paintballs by pressing \"Refill 20 Paintballs\" button or saying the voice command \"Refill Paint Ball\". Try to move around to dodge incoming paintballs, or teleport to reposition. Score by reducing others' health bars to zero, upon which they would enter ghost mode and respawn at a random location in 10 seconds. \r\n\r\nIn Immersive headsets: Make sure you set up boundary for all experiences before you begin. While \"Painting On\", once you see your robotic right hand holding a paint brush, you can press the right hand trigger button to start drawing. While \"Paint Balling\", you can aim with your right hand controller, and press right hand trigger to shoot paintballs.\r\n\r\nOnce you see your robotic left arm holding a motion controller, you can use the touch pad to select paint color. Alternatively, you can tap \"Pick Color\" to bring up the large color wheel. \r\n\r\nIf you made a mistake, you can say \"Erase Last Stroke\" or press right hand controller grab button. You can also clear all strokes by saying \"Erase All Strokes\". \r\n\r\nTo rotate your view, point the joysticks left or right on one of the motion controllers. \r\n\r\nTo teleport, make sure the panel shows \"Teleport On\". Then point your cursor at the floor with one of the motion controllers, and hold the joystick forward until a Teleport marker appears, then release the joystick. \r\n\r\nIn HoloLens, you can use gaze, tap gesture to select options on the menu in front of you (look below chest level). You can use the same voice commands as elaborated above. While \"Painting On\", you can reach your hand out in front of you, pinch and hold while dragging the paint brush along. While \"Paint Balling\", you can aim with your gaze and air tap to shoot paintballs.\r\n\r\nBefore teleporting in HoloLens, make sure the panel shows \"Teleport On\". Then you can use your gaze to aim, and then tap to dash across the map! You could also hide the Guessing Window and the Panel if they are blocking your gazes. Remember to turn off teleport before drawing or shooting. \r\n\r\n\r\n","ProductFamilyName":"Games","Schema":"Card;1"}],"Title":"Beliebteste","HasThirdPartyIAPs":false,"AlgoName":"RECO-Algo-Version","TotalItems":987,"PageSize":200}}
